1.3.1 Informasjon og relasjoner (4 avvik)
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

First heading is h2, should start with h1

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center animated fadeInUp" style="font-style:normal;font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase">Vi jobber for fiskeren</h2>
Start your heading structure with h1
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Heading level skipped: h2 to h4

<h4>Tar opp saksbehandlingstid</h4>
Don't skip heading levels. Use h3 instead of h4
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Heading level skipped: h2 to h4

<h4 class="show-for-large">Kontakt</h4>
Don't skip heading levels. Use h3 instead of h4
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Page has 2 main landmarks (should have 1)

<main>
